(function() {
    var href = document.location.href;
    var siteUrl = window.location.port ? window.location.protocol+'//'+window.location.hostname +':'+window.location.port : window.location.protocol+'//'+window.location.hostname;
    var hash = window.location.hash;
    if ( hash && hash.indexOf( '&_suid' ) !== -1 )  {
        var pieces = hash.split( '&_suid' );
        var pieces2 = pieces[0].replace( '#', '' );
        if ( pieces2.indexOf( '.' ) === 0 ) {
            pieces2 = pieces2.replace( '.', '' );
        }
        if ( pieces2.indexOf( '/' ) === 0 ) {
            pieces2 = pieces2.replace( '/', '' );
        }
        if ( pieces2.indexOf( '?' ) === pieces2.length -1 ) {
            pieces2 = pieces2.replace( '?', '' );
        }
        window.location.replace( siteUrl + '/' + (unescape(pieces2.replace(/\+/g, " "))));
    } else if ( hash && hash.indexOf( '!state' ) !== -1 ) {
        var pieces = hash.split( '__' );
      if ( pieces.length > 1 ) {
        window.location.replace( siteUrl + '/' + (unescape(pieces[1].replace(/\+/g, " "))));
      }
    }
})();

    var uuid = uuidv4();
    if ( uuid ) {
        return uuid;
    } else {
        var a = function(c) {
            var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
            return v.toString(16);
        }
        return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, a);
    }
};
